		"articleBody": " In a way, Captain America: Civil War turned out to be Black Panther&#039;s film as much as anyone&#039;s. The newly introduced Prince T&#039;Challa – as played by Chadwick Boseman – might not have scored the most screen time, but he was the hero who really seemed changed by Iron Man and Cap&#039;s showdown. Marvel Studios is great at many things, but not so much at diversity, so Black Panther also marks the first solo film not starring a white dude. Suffice to say, we&#039;re very excited about the movie. Here&#039;s the rundown on what to expect when T&#039;Challa goes on the warpath. Black Panther cast: Young and gifted  Creed and Fruitvale Station director Ryan Coogler is taking the reins of Black Panther for Marvel, and he&#039;s gathering a cast of talented young black actors for the movie. Get On Up and... er... Gods of Egypt star Boseman is of course back as the recently orphaned prince of the fictional and scientifically advanced African nation Wakanda. Although we suppose he&#039;s king now.  Coogler is bringing his frequent collaborator Michael B Jordan along for the ride. It was revealed at San Diego Comic-Con 2016 that he will be playing the magnificently named Erik Killmonger, a Wakandan exile with a grudge against his former king, T&#039;Challa. (Just nobody mention Fantastic Four, please.) Star Wars: The Force Awakens star Lupita Nyong&#039;o is also on board to play a Wakandan called Nakia. In the comics, she was a member of the royal bodyguard called the Dora Milaje, but was kicked out for becoming obsessed with Black Panther and trying to kill his lover. She hooked up with Killmonger and gained supernatural powers as the villain Malice. Killmonger and Malice. Not at all on the nose, right?  Danai Gurira – best known as The Walking Dead&#039;s Michonne – will play Okoye, another Dora Milaje – albeit one who doesn&#039;t betray her king. Forest Whitaker will be following up Rogue One: A Star Wars Story by playing Zuri, an &#039;elder statesman&#039; of Wakanda, with Florence Kasumba, Daniel Kaluuya (Black Mirror), Winston Duke (Person of Interest) and Letitia Wright (Doctor Who, My Brother the Devil) also on board. This is Us actor Sterling K Brown will appear as N&#039;Jobu, &quot;a figure from T&#039;Challa&#039;s... past&quot;. The legendary Angela Bassett (American Horror Story, What&#039;s Love Got to Do with It) will appear as T&#039;Challa&#039;s mother, the queen mother of Wakanda. Andy Serkis is back as classic Black Panther foe Ulysses Klaw – who Killmonger also despises for enslaving his family. It&#039;s not official yet, but it would be very strange to have awkwardly introduced Klaw in Avengers: Age of Ultron just to leave him on the shelf.      So I took some great shots of #AndySerkis filming #BlackPanther... haven&#039;t seen them yet. Here is one not-so-great to hold you over. pic.twitter.com/0YlYfNqRTS — Atlanta Filming (@AtlantaFilming) February 8, 2017    Martin Freeman will reprise his role as Everett Ross, Deputy Task Force Commander of the Joint Counter Terrorist Centre from Captain America: Civil War. Samuel L Jackson wanted to bring back Nick Fury, but was told &#039;no&#039;. We&#039;ll probably have to wait for Avengers: Infinity War for his return. Sebastian Stan&#039;s Winter Soldier – who is currently on ice in Wakanda – is seemingly back for Infinity War. Could we see he thawed out ahead of time in Black Panther?  Marvel is also looking to cast people of African heritage from 18 to 90-years-old, particularly people with skills in drumming, MMA and wrestling. Piercings and shaved heads welcome all round. It sounds like Wakanda&#039;s going to be a diverse (and militaristic) place.  Black Panther plot: Civil War aftermath        Not much has been revealed at this point, although Nyong&#039;o did apparently let slip more than she should have at Comic-Con. &quot;The story of this Black Panther is – what am I allowed to say? – that the Black Panther&#039;s leadership is really threatened by two foes who come together, and so Black Panther gets the help of the CIA and the Dora Milaje to try and defeat the enemy,&quot; she said. Since then, we&#039;ve had the full synopsis: &quot;Black Panther follows T&#039;Challa who, after the events of Captain America: Civil War, returns home to the isolated, technologically advanced African nation of Wakanda to take his place as King. However, when an old enemy reappears on the radar, T&#039;Challa&#039;s mettle as King and Black Panther is tested when he is drawn into a conflict that puts the entire fate of Wakanda and the world at risk.&quot; There have also been some hints at a &#039;90s flashback. The film feels like the next best chance to pick up the threads from Civil War, with the Avengers divided and Cap&#039;s team last seen hanging out in Wakanda, while T&#039;Challa gets to grips with his new role as king. That&#039;s looking very likely after writer Joe Robert Cole that Black Panther is set shortly after Marvel&#039;s 2015 movie.  So we would expect some cameos from Cap and co, or at least some acknowledgement of what is going on in the wider MCU. And we don&#039;t think the crown is going to stand in the way of Black Panther donning his badass bulletproof costume and putting some bad guys in their place. Boseman has said that it will be &quot;grittier&quot; than your average MCU film, and has described his character as an &quot;anti-hero&quot; (well, an &quot;anti-superhero&quot;). And having a majority black cast for a major blockbuster might be a landmark moment, but he&#039;s trying not to think about it while he&#039;s shooting. Black Panther release date: In the shadow of Infinity War        Shooting begins in early 2017, and Boseman&#039;s solo outing lands at an increasingly busy time in Marvel&#039;s schedule. It will be released in the UK on February 9, 2018, and in the US on February 16, 2018. That puts it only three months before the first instalment of the two-part Avengers: Infinity War film, adding to our anticipation about how it will tie into the next big Marvel team-up and the overall story of the MCU. 				<div class="shop-item--button" class="<%= ( product.status === 'out_of_stock') ? 'sold-out' : ''%> ">
					<i class="icon icon-cart"></i>
					<span><%= product.buttonLabel %></span>
				</div>
			</div>
		</a>
		<% if ( product.hasReviews ) { %>
			<div class="js-modal-show" data-modal-id="modal-reviews" data-review-href="<%= product.reviewsHref %>">
				<%= product.reviewsLabel %>
			</div>
		<% } %>

	<% } else if ( products.length > 1 ) { %>
	<!-- multi-shop -->
		<ul class="shop-products">
			<% _.forEach(products, function(product) { %>
			<li class="shop-products--results" data-id="<%= product.count %>">
				<a href="<%= product.href %>"
				   class="shop-item--wrap"
				   data-product-name="<%= product.name %>"
				   target="_blank"
				>
					<div class="shop-item">
						<% if ( product.image ) { %>
							<div class="shop-item--image" href="" target="_blank">
								<img src="<%= product.image %>" data-large="<%=product.largeImage%>" class="lazy-image" />
							</div>
						<% } %>
					</div>
					<div class="shop-item--controls">
						<div class="shop-item--button-wrap">
							<div class="shop-item--button" class="<%= ( product.status === 'out_of_stock') ? 'sold-out' : ''%> ">
								<i class="icon icon-cart"></i>
								<span><%= product.buttonLabel %></span>
							</div>

						<% var productBrandName = (product.brand || product.name) %>
						<% if (productBrandName) { %>
							<div class="shop-item--designer"><%= productBrandName %></div>
						<% } %>

						</div>

					</div>
				</a>
			</li>
			<% }); %>
		</ul>
	<% } %></script> <div
class="modal-overlay product-modal-overlay"><div
id="modal-reviews" class="modal">

		<div class="modal-shop--product-image-inner">
			<% if ( typeof largeImage !== "undefined") { %>
				<img src="<%=largeImage%>">
			<% } else { %>
				<img src="<%=image%>">
			<% } %>
		</div>
	</div>
	<div class="modal-shop--product-name">
		<span><%=name%></span>
	</div>
	<div class="modal-shop--button-wrap">
		<a href="<%=href%>"
		   target="_blank"
		   data-product-name="<%= name %>"
		>
			<div class="modal-shop--product-button">
				<span><%= buttonLabel %></span>
			</div>

class="standard-article-body--text"><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">In a way, <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor"><a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/captain-america/review/a791330/captain-america-civil-war-review-the-most-grown-up-super-hero-movie-yet/">Captain America: Civil War</a></em> turned out to be Black Panther's film as much as anyone's. <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/captain-america/news/a790984/black-panther-wasnt-even-going-to-get-a-costume-in-captain-america-civil-war/">The newly introduced Prince T'Challa</a> &ndash; as played by Chadwick Boseman &ndash; might not have scored the most screen time, but he was the hero who really seemed changed by Iron Man and Cap's showdown.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Marvel Studios is great at many things, but not so much at diversity, so <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Black Panther</em> also marks the first solo film not starring a white dude.</p><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker-container"><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker ad-article-breaker-mobile " data-id="gpt-ad-vertical-top-mobile"><div
class="ad-article-breaker-text">Advertisement - Continue Reading Below</div><div
class="gpt-tag" id="gpt-ad-vertical-top-mobile"></div></div></div><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Suffice to say, we're very excited about the movie. Here's the rundown on what to expect when T'Challa goes on the warpath.</p><h4 class="question body-el-question standard-body-el-question">Black Panther cast: Young and gifted</h4><div

class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"><em

<span

class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Coogler is bringing his frequent collaborator Michael B Jordan along for the ride. It was revealed at <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/news/a802361/black-panther-new-logo-casting-announcements-comic-con-2016/">San Diego Comic-Con 2016</a> that he will be playing the magnificently named Erik Killmonger, a Wakandan exile with a grudge against his former king, T'Challa. (Just nobody mention <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/fantastic-four/news/a780136/michael-b-jordan-is-standing-by-fantastic-four-despite-box-office-flop/"><em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Fantastic Four</em></a>, please.)</p><div
class="ad-article-breaker standard-article-body-el-breaker"><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker-container"><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker mobile-only " data-id="ad-article-breaker-mobile-0"><div
class="ad-article-breaker-text">Advertisement - Continue Reading Below</div><div
class="gpt-tag" id="ad-article-breaker-mobile-0"></div></div></div></div><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"><em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Star Wars: The Force Awakens</em> star Lupita Nyong'o is also on board to play a Wakandan called Nakia. In the comics, she was a member of the royal bodyguard called the Dora Milaje, but was kicked out for becoming obsessed with Black Panther and trying to kill his lover. She hooked up with Killmonger and gained supernatural powers as the villain Malice.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Killmonger and Malice. Not at all on the nose, right?</p><div

class="image-copyright">
<span
class="image-copyright--symbol">&copy;</span>&nbsp;
<span
class="image-copyright--provider">Marvel Studios</span></div></div></div><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Danai Gurira &ndash; best known as <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">The Walking Dead</em>'s Michonne &ndash; will play Okoye, another Dora Milaje &ndash; albeit one who doesn't betray her king. <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a810400/oscar-winner-forest-whitaker-jumps-from-rogue-one-a-star-wars-story-to-marvels-black-panther/" target="_blank">Forest Whitaker</a> will be following up <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/star-wars/feature/a649674/rogue-one-a-star-wars-story-trailer-cast-plot-release-date-and-everything-you-need-to-know/" target="_blank"><em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Rogue One: A Star Wars Story</em></a> by playing Zuri, an 'elder statesman' of Wakanda, with Florence Kasumba, Daniel Kaluuya (<em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Black Mirror</em>), Winston Duke (<em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Person of Interest</em>) and Letitia Wright (<em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Doctor Who</em>, <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">My Brother the Devil</em>) also on board. <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">This is Us</em> actor Sterling K Brown will appear as N'Jobu, "a figure from T'Challa's... past".</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">The legendary <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a814785/american-horror-storys-angela-bassett-marvels-black-panther/" target="_blank">Angela Bassett</a> (<em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">American Horror Story</em>, <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">What's Love Got to Do with It</em>) will appear as T'Challa's mother, the queen mother of Wakanda.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"><a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a819927/black-panther-bringing-back-major-marvel-villain-unveils-synopsis/" target="_blank" data-tracking-id="recirc-text-link">Andy Serkis</a> is back as classic Black Panther foe Ulysses Klaw &ndash; who Killmonger also despises for enslaving his family. It's not official yet, but it would be very strange to have awkwardly introduced Klaw in <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Avengers: Age of Ultron</em> just to leave him on the shelf.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"></p><div
class="embed embed--center embed--twitter"><div
class="embed--inner"><blockquote
class=""><p
lang="en" dir="ltr">So I took some great shots of <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/AndySerkis?src=hash">#AndySerkis</a> filming <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/BlackPanther?src=hash">#BlackPanther</a>... haven't seen them yet. Here is one not-so-great to hold you over. <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="https://t.co/0YlYfNqRTS">pic.twitter.com/0YlYfNqRTS</a></p><p>&mdash; Atlanta Filming (@AtlantaFilming) <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="https://twitter.com/AtlantaFilming/status/829136933267857409">February 8, 2017</a></p></blockquote></div></div></div><div
class="ad-article-breaker standard-article-body-el-breaker"><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker-container"><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker  " data-id="ad-article-breaker-leaderboard-0"><div
class="ad-article-breaker-text">Advertisement - Continue Reading Below</div><div
class="gpt-tag" id="ad-article-breaker-leaderboard-0"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div
class="standard-article-body--container standard-article-body--container-main"><div
class="standard-article--secondary-content ad-article-breaker"><div
class="standard-article--primary-ad " data-id="gpt-ad-vertical-top-0"><div
class="ad-gpt-main"><div
class="gpt-tag " id="gpt-ad-vertical-top-0"></div></div></div></div><div
class="standard-article-body--content"><div
class="standard-article-body--text"><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"><a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a819719/martin-freeman-black-panther-evert-k-ross-marvel-movie-captain-america-civil-war/" target="_blank" data-tracking-id="recirc-text-link">Martin Freeman</a> will reprise his role as Everett Ross, Deputy Task Force Commander of the Joint Counter Terrorist Centre from <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Captain America: Civil War</em>.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Samuel L Jackson wanted to bring back <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a821663/samuel-l-jackson-nick-fury-in-black-panther/" target="_blank" data-tracking-id="recirc-text-link">Nick Fury</a>, but was told 'no'. We'll probably have to wait for <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor"><a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/the-avengers/news/a804280/the-winter-soldier-confirmed-for-avengers-infinity-war/">Avengers: Infinity War</a></em> for his return.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Sebastian Stan's Winter Soldier &ndash; who is currently on ice in Wakanda &ndash; is seemingly back for <em
data-verified="redactor" data-redactor-tag="em">Infinity War</em>. Could we see he thawed out ahead of time in <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Black Panther</em>?</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"> Marvel is also looking to cast people of <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.tammysmithcasting.com/TSCasting/Casting_Notices.html">African heritage from 18 to 90-years-old</a>, particularly people with skills in drumming, MMA and wrestling. Piercings and shaved heads welcome all round. It sounds like Wakanda's going to be a diverse (and militaristic) place.</p><h4 class="question body-el-question standard-body-el-question">Black Panther plot: Civil War aftermath</h4><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"></p><div
class="embed embed--left embed--giphy embed--generic embed--lazy-iframe"><div
class="embed--inner"><div
class="embed--iframe-container" style="padding-bottom: 56.25%;"><iframe
data-src="//giphy.com/embed/doUNGqZL7G89O" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" allowtransparency="true"></iframe></div></div></div><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Not much has been revealed at this point, although Nyong'o did apparently let slip <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/news/a802624/black-panther-villain-details-revealed-by-lupita-nyongo/">more than she should have</a> at Comic-Con.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">"The story of this Black Panther is &ndash; what am I allowed to say? &ndash; that the Black Panther's leadership is really threatened by two foes who come together, and so Black Panther gets the help of the CIA and the Dora Milaje to try and defeat the enemy," she said.</p><div
class="ad-article-breaker standard-article-body-el-breaker"><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker-container"><div
class="ad-gpt-breaker mobile-only " data-id="ad-article-breaker-mobile-1"><div
class="ad-article-breaker-text">Advertisement - Continue Reading Below</div><div
class="gpt-tag" id="ad-article-breaker-mobile-1"></div></div></div></div><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Since then, we've had the full synopsis:</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">"<em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Black Panther</em> follows T'Challa who, after the events of <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Captain America: Civil War</em>, returns home to the isolated, technologically advanced African nation of Wakanda to take his place as King. However, when an old enemy reappears on the radar, T'Challa's mettle as King and Black Panther is tested when he is drawn into a conflict that puts the entire fate of Wakanda and the world at risk."</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">There have also been some hints at a <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a819213/marvel-black-panther-90s-flashback-confirmed/" target="_blank" data-tracking-id="recirc-text-link">'90s flashback</a>.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">The film feels like the next best chance to pick up the threads from <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor"><a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/captain-america/feature/a792055/how-captain-america-civil-war-sets-up-marvel-phase-3-future/">Civil War</a></em>, with the Avengers divided and Cap's team last seen hanging out in Wakanda, while T'Challa gets to grips with his new role as king. That's looking very likely after writer Joe Robert Cole that <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor">Black Panther</em> is <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/captain-america/news/a804739/black-panther-starts-directly-after-captain-america-civil-war/">set shortly after Marvel's 2015 movie</a>.</p><div
class="embedded-image  embedded-image--CM standard-article-embedded-image--CM standard-article-body-el-image"><div
class="embedded-image--inner">

<span

class="image-copyright--provider">Marvel Studios</span></div></div></div><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">So we would expect some cameos from Cap and co, or at least some acknowledgement of what is going on in the wider MCU. And we don't think the crown is going to stand in the way of Black Panther donning his badass bulletproof costume and putting some bad guys in their place.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Boseman has said that it will be <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a806930/black-panther-could-be-marvels-grittiest-film-yet/" target="_blank">"grittier"</a> than your average MCU film, and has described his character as an <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.comicbookmovie.com/black_panther/black-panther-star-chadwick-boseman-refers-to-his-take-on-tchalla-a145127" target="_blank">"anti-hero"</a> (well, an "anti-superhero"). And having a majority black cast for a major blockbuster might be a landmark moment, but <a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/black-panther/news/a807827/black-panther-chadwick-boseman-cant-think-about-how-big-the-movie-will-be/" target="_blank">he's trying not to think about it while he's shooting</a>.</p><h4 class="question body-el-question standard-body-el-question">Black Panther release date: In the shadow of Infinity War</h4><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"></p><div
class="embed embed--left embed--giphy embed--generic embed--lazy-iframe"><div
class="embed--inner"><div
class="embed--iframe-container" style="padding-bottom: 61.041666666667%;"><iframe
data-src="//giphy.com/embed/IM9wxMhbgRRF6" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" allowtransparency="true"></iframe></div></div></div><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">Shooting begins in early 2017, and Boseman's solo outing lands at an increasingly busy time in Marvel's schedule. It will be released in the UK on February 9, 2018, and in the US on February 16, 2018.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text">That puts it only three months before the first instalment of the two-part <em
data-redactor-tag="em" data-verified="redactor"><a
class="body-el-link standard-body-el-link" href="http://www.digitalspy.com/movies/the-avengers/feature/a790651/avengers-infinity-war-part-1-and-2-cast-release-date-plot-spoilers-and-everything-you-need-to-know/">Avengers: Infinity War</a></em> film, adding to our anticipation about how it will tie into the next big Marvel team-up and the overall story of the MCU.</p><p
class="body-el-text standard-body-el-text"></p><div
class="embed embed--center embed--twitter"><div

<a
